        <a title="Linda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Linda" href="/user/show/3919132-linda">Linda</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3919132-linda?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3919132-linda?shelf=contemporary-paranormal">contemporary-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3919132-linda?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3919132-linda?shelf=dark-paranormal">dark-paranormal</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer115486829" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16945096052270773968">Ciara Griffin is a former con artist turned radio station intern. Trying to mend her ways she takes a job at WVMP and dives into the secret world of vampires and Control, the agency who keeps the world safe. <br/><br/>These vampires really need to drink daily but can survive longer and they can use banked blood but prefer fresh donors. The big difference is that these vampires are locked in the specific time when they became the undead and their mind is stagnant. Supposedly they have an impossible time le</span>
  <span id="freeText16945096052270773968" style="display:none">Ciara Griffin is a former con artist turned radio station intern. Trying to mend her ways she takes a job at WVMP and dives into the secret world of vampires and Control, the agency who keeps the world safe. <br /><br />These vampires really need to drink daily but can survive longer and they can use banked blood but prefer fresh donors. The big difference is that these vampires are locked in the specific time when they became the undead and their mind is stagnant. Supposedly they have an impossible time learning new things to keep them moving continually towards the future. After so long, they eventually morph into something that is blah and slide into oblivion. Lastly, if they should be killed and not 'die' on their own their death is worse than horrible. <br /><br />Ciara eventually falls for Shane McAllister, one of the vamps. Besides living vs. dead there is plenty of angst with their relationship. Shane was by no means perfect in his former life and Ciara is carrying a big package herself. Still, they play well off each other and you want good things to happen. There are several secondary stories that keep the book moving along. <br /><br />Tidbits about songs filter throughout and you will probably enjoy this if you grew up in the 80s or are a music lover. If this is your type of story you will probably enjoy 'Covet', another dark paranormal book and the first in a new series by J. R. Ward. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16945096052270773968" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_120197655" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/120197655" />
    <a title="Lori Whitwam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/715797-lori-whitwam"><img alt="Lori Whitwam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442535080p2/715797.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/120197655?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lori Whitwam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lori Whitwam" href="/user/show/715797-lori-whitwam">Lori Whitwam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/715797-lori-whitwam?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/715797-lori-whitwam?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/715797-lori-whitwam?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer120197655" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7337325995962376261">A happy surprise. So many paranormal/urban fantasy are so similar that it's hard to tell one series from another. But... Ciara's new vampire buds are unique. In this world, vampires are "locked" into the time in which they died. Handy here, since they are all DJs, specializing in the music of their decade. They can't really assimilate new information into their worldview, such as the 60s character can see and theoretically understand the use of computers, but can't incorporate it into his life. </span>
  <span id="freeText7337325995962376261" style="display:none">A happy surprise. So many paranormal/urban fantasy are so similar that it's hard to tell one series from another. But... Ciara's new vampire buds are unique. In this world, vampires are "locked" into the time in which they died. Handy here, since they are all DJs, specializing in the music of their decade. They can't really assimilate new information into their worldview, such as the 60s character can see and theoretically understand the use of computers, but can't incorporate it into his life. The conflict of the world changing around them causes many to develop control-coping mechanisms, in the form of obsessive-compulsive behaviors. <br /><br />So, Ciara brings the vampires "out" as a marketing ploy to save the struggling station. Hide in plain sight... nobody will believe it. Except the leader of a crazy cult of isolationist vampires who fear exposure.<br /><br />The author's voice is smart and funny, including numerous lines I had to share with friends. Too clever! I've already downloaded book 2, and am starting it... right now!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7337325995962376261" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sy0P3pYh+ICGlGdKHNBc6GtcTabqLbfjFyalDVLkUlSnquaerjKXA9mTApnJA4EOKf9Q/uGXwrls+hcfw5FE3A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kwUtlzcnkWNfVBR9N2f/Le2aY8PBUK4x9e6ORRLMO1CHgsTXDzT+4ABTca7itCLLrzl+m8rq22uOMjxXg7kt2A==')})
  }

A steady stream of caffeine has produced twelve published novels for teens and adults since 2001.<br/><br/>Jeri lives in Maryland with her husband and two cats, who often play tag-team "sit in the author's lap and keep her from writing." It’s Ciara’s job to keep the undead rocking, the ratings rolling, and the fan base alive—without missing a beat.\n\nFor Halloween, WVMP is throwing a bash sure to raise the dead. They’ve got cool tunes, hot costumes, killer cocktails—what could go wrong? Well, for starters, a religious firebrand ranting against the evils of the occult preempts the station’s midnight broadcast.
